<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскланяться.html>раскла́няться</a> (18740)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кланяться.html>кла́няться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klánjatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскланяться.html>раскла́няться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasklánjatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскланиваться.html>раскла́ниваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bow <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of a gentleman or performer</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to greet by bowing <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say goodbye, to bid farewell</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскованность.html>раско́ванность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskóvannostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскованность.html>раско́ванности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскованность.html>раско́ванности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскованность.html>раско́ванностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>relaxedness, uninhibitedness</li></ol>

***раскол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскол.html>раско́л</a> (15399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Action noun of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расколоть.html>расколо́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raskolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскол.html>раско́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскол.html>раско́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскол.html>раско́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расколоть.html>раско́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>split, dissidence</li>
<li>cleavage</li>
<li>disunity</li>
<li>schism, dissent</li></ol>

***расколоть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расколоть.html>расколо́ть</a> (10853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расколоть.html>расколо́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskolótʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскалывать.html>раска́лывать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to split, to cleave, to break <i>(sugar)</i>, to crack <i>(nuts)</i>, to chop <i>(firewood)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to divide, to split up
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскалывать.html>раска́лывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raskályvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make to talk</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расколоть.html>расколо́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raskolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расколоться.html>расколо́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskolótʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскалываться.html>раска́лываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cleave, to split, to crack</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start talking, to tell/reveal/disclose the truth, to blab, to let it out, to spill the beans, to spill</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расколоть.html>расколо́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raskolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 10c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:раскалываться.html>раска́лываться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>рас-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-кол-</b>; суффикс: <b>-о</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскопать.html>раско́панный</a> (18827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскопать.html>раско́панный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskópannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскопать.html>раскопа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raskopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>пан</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>Прича́стие</a>.

***раскопать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскопать.html>раскопа́ть</a> (18827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копать.html>копа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскопать.html>раскопа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskopátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскапывать.html>раска́пывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dig out, to grub up, to grub out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dig out, to dig up, to unearth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полиция.html>поли́ция</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раскопать.html>раскопа́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>сведения</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">polícija <b>raskopála</b> nóvyje svedenija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the police have unearthed [dug up] new information</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раскопать.html>раскопа́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюки.html>брю́ки</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gde ty <b>raskopál</b> éti brjúki?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">where did you dig up these trousers?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archeology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to excavate</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскосый.html>раско́сый</a> (17466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коса.html>косо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kosój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскосый.html>раско́сый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskósyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)раско́сее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)раско́сей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slant-eyed</li>
<li>suffering from strabismus, cross-eyed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> slanted, inclined, oblique</li></ol>

***раскошелиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскошелиться.html>раскоше́литься</a> (25400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">коше́ль</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">košélʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">purse (dated)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскошелиться.html>раскоше́литься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskošélitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раскоше́ливаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be cough up (money), to shell out (money)</li></ol>

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:краснеть.html>красне́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krasnétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскроить.html>раскрои́ть</a> (30531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроить.html>крои́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kroítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскроить.html>раскрои́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskroítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроить.html>крои́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раскра́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut out (fabric to specific lengths and shapes to make clothes)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>и́ть</b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрыть.html>раскро́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskrój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрой.html>раскро́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрой.html>раскро́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрой.html>раскро́ев</a></b>)

***раскрутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ть</a> (19132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">разкрꙋтити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razkrutiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orzkrǫtiti</i>. Morphologically <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskrutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскручивать.html>раскру́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to unwind, to unroll, to unspin
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковёр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raskrutítʹ</b> kovjór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>roll out</b> the carpet</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to promote, to market, to hype
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сайт.html>сайт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> Google</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>raskrutítʹ</b> svoj sajt v Google</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how to <b>make</b> your site have a <b>good ranking</b> in Google search results</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to persuade someone into doing something (often with deceit), to hustle someone into doing something/out of their money, etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:французский.html>францу́зские</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:журналист.html>журнали́сты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сексуальный.html>сексуа́льную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:актриса.html>актри́су</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небольшой.html>небольшо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:эксперимент.html>экспериме́нт</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Francúzskije žurnalísty <b>raskrutíli</b> sɛksuálʹnuju aktrísu na nebolʹšój eksperimént.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">French journalists (photographers) <b>persuaded</b> the sexy actress to do a little experiment.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">стриптизёрша "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ла</a></b>" <a href = vnd.unilang:клиент.html>клие́нта</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> 100 <a href = vnd.unilang:доллар.html>до́лларов</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">striptizjórša "<b>raskrutíla</b>" klijénta na 100 dóllarov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the stripper "<b>took</b>" the client for 100 dollars / the stripper <b>hustled</b> the client out of 100 dollars total</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскрученный.html>раскру́ченный</a> (19132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрученный.html>раскру́ченный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskrúčennyj</span>)

***раскручивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскручивать.html>раскру́чивать</a> (20659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raskrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскручивать.html>раскру́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskrúčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to unwind, to unroll, to unspin
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раскручивать.html>раскру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковёр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raskrúčivatʹ</b> kovjór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>roll out</b> the carpet</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to promote, to market, to hype</li>
<li>to persuade someone into doing something (often with deceit), to hustle someone into doing something/out of their money, etc.</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кру́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:раскрутить.html>раскрути́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>рас-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-круч-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ива</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раскручиваться.html>раскру́чиваться</a> (26488)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскручивать.html>раскру́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raskrúčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскручиваться.html>раскру́чиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raskrúčivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раскрути́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unwind, to untwist, to unscrew</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spin <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">strongly</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to succeed in business, to become well-known <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">through business</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскручивать.html>раскру́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raskrúčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
